\section{Behavorial}\label{behavorial}

\subsection{Overall scores}\label{overall-scores}

The tables show performance and reaction time statistics per participant
and per age group.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{ttestfromMeans <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(cdata)}
\NormalTok{\{}
  \NormalTok{df <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cdata$n[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] +}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cdata$n[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{] -}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}
  \NormalTok{poolvar <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(((cdata$n[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] -}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) *}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cdata$sd[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]^}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) +}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{              }\NormalTok{((cdata$n[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{] -}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) *}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cdata$sd[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{]^}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{))/df}
  \NormalTok{t <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(cdata$m[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] -}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cdata$m[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{]) /}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{    }\KeywordTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{(poolvar *}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{((}\DecValTok{1} \NormalTok{/}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cdata$n[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]) +}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{                    }\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1} \NormalTok{/}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cdata$n[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{])))}
  \NormalTok{sig<-}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{*(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{-(}\KeywordTok{pt}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{abs}\NormalTok{(t),df)))}
  \KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df: "}\NormalTok{, df, }\StringTok{", t: "}\NormalTok{, }
      \KeywordTok{round}\NormalTok{(t, }\DataTypeTok{digits =} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{", sig: "}\NormalTok{, }
      \KeywordTok{round}\NormalTok{(sig, }\DataTypeTok{digits =} \DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\CommentTok{# Read multiple log files}

\NormalTok{log <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{log[}\KeywordTok{complete.cases}\NormalTok{(log),]}
\NormalTok{log$id <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(log$id)}

\CommentTok{# Sys.setlocale("LC_ALL", "German_Germany")}
\CommentTok{# Sys.setlocale(category = "LC_ALL", locale = "English_United States.1252")}

\CommentTok{# # convert to POSIXct to use in data frames / ddply}

\NormalTok{data <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{log}

\CommentTok{# YA vs OA}
\NormalTok{data$age_group <-}\StringTok{ "young"}
\NormalTok{data$age_group[data$age >}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{50}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "old"}

\CommentTok{# determine if participant started the experiment with a block with 8 or 4 options}
\CommentTok{# participants with an uneven id started with 4 options}
\NormalTok{data$block_size_start <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}
\NormalTok{data$block_size_start[}\KeywordTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(data$id)) %%}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2} \NormalTok{==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4} 

\CommentTok{# block_id: block 1-16 }
\CommentTok{# determine the block size in the current block}
\CommentTok{# first, set all block sizes the same as the first}
\NormalTok{data$block_size <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$block_size_start }
\CommentTok{# participants who started with 8, have 4 options in even block ids}
\CommentTok{# participants who started with 4, have 8 options in even block ids}
\NormalTok{data$block_size[data$block_id %%}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2} \NormalTok{==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$block_size_start ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}
\NormalTok{data$block_size[data$block_id %%}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2} \NormalTok{==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$block_size_start ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}

\CommentTok{# look up which of the fixed 16 unique problems a participant is solving}
\CommentTok{# every 3rd and 4th participant have an increasing problem order }
\CommentTok{# every 1st and 2nd participant have a  decreasing problem order }
\CommentTok{# do id-1 to do check <2}
\NormalTok{data$block_order <-}\StringTok{ "dec"}
\CommentTok{# (unique(as.integer(as.character(data$id))-1) %% 4)}
\NormalTok{data$check <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(((}\KeywordTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(data$id))-}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) %%}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{) <}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{T }
\NormalTok{data$block_order[data$check] <-}\StringTok{ "inc"}
\NormalTok{data$block_order <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(data$block_order)}

\CommentTok{# determine problem id independent of increasing or decreasing}
\NormalTok{data$real_block_id <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$block_id}
\CommentTok{# decreasing block orders always started at problem number 10 }
\NormalTok{data$real_block_id[data$block_order ==}\StringTok{ "dec"}\NormalTok{] =}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{10} \NormalTok{-}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{    }\NormalTok{(data$block_id[data$block_order ==}\StringTok{ "dec"}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{data$real_block_id[data$real_block_id <=}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{] =}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{16} \NormalTok{+}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{    }\NormalTok{(data$real_block_id[data$real_block_id <=}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{])}

\CommentTok{# subtract 1 from identified problem id's for pp who start with 8 options}
\CommentTok{# every problem id has a seperate file for both block sizes }
\CommentTok{# (which are actually the same)}

\NormalTok{agg =}\StringTok{ "id"} \CommentTok{# grouping var}

\CommentTok{# calc speeds}
\NormalTok{cdata.speed <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{aggregate}\NormalTok{(data[}\StringTok{"rt"}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{by=}\NormalTok{data[}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"block_id"}\NormalTok{, agg)], }\DataTypeTok{FUN=}\NormalTok{sum)}

\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.speed.m)[}\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.speed.m)==}\StringTok{"speed"}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "sp.m"}

\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.speed.sd)[}\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.speed.sd)==}\StringTok{"speed"}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "sp.sd"}

\CommentTok{# cdata.sp}

\CommentTok{# age}
\NormalTok{cdata.group <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{ddply}\NormalTok{(data, .(id), summarize, }
                     \DataTypeTok{age_group =} \NormalTok{age_group[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{],}
                     \DataTypeTok{age =} \NormalTok{age[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{cdata.sp <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{merge}\NormalTok{(cdata.sp, cdata.group)}

\CommentTok{# blocks}
\NormalTok{blocks <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data[data$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{max}\NormalTok{(data$trial_number),]}

\CommentTok{# calc avg score per pp across blocks}
\NormalTok{cdata.n <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{aggregate}\NormalTok{(blocks[}\StringTok{"block_score"}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{by=}\NormalTok{blocks[}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(agg)], }\DataTypeTok{FUN=}\NormalTok{length)}
\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.n)[}\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.n)==}\StringTok{"block_score"}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "n"}
\NormalTok{cdata.m <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{aggregate}\NormalTok{(blocks[}\StringTok{"block_score"}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{by=}\NormalTok{blocks[}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(agg)], }\DataTypeTok{FUN=}\NormalTok{mean)}
\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.m)[}\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.m)==}\StringTok{"block_score"}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "m"}
\NormalTok{cdata.sd <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{aggregate}\NormalTok{(blocks[}\StringTok{"block_score"}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{by=}\NormalTok{blocks[}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(agg)], }\DataTypeTok{FUN=}\NormalTok{sd)}
\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.sd)[}\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cdata.sd)==}\StringTok{"block_score"}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "sd"}
\NormalTok{cdata <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{merge}\NormalTok{(cdata.n, cdata.m)}
\NormalTok{cdata <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{merge}\NormalTok{(cdata, cdata.sd)}
\NormalTok{cdata$se <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cdata$sd /}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{(cdata$n)}
\NormalTok{cdata <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{merge}\NormalTok{(cdata, cdata.sp)}

  \CommentTok{# time spent on reading information}

  \NormalTok{reading <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(reading,}\KeywordTok{difftime}\NormalTok{(inftrial$timestrip, lastplaintrial$timestrip, }\DataTypeTok{unit=}\StringTok{"secs"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{\}}
\CommentTok{# time spent on first information trial}
\NormalTok{inftrial <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{log[log$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{log$block_id ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{9}\NormalTok{,] }
\KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(reading) <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{inftrial$age}
\end{Highlighting}

  significant performance difference for the 8 conditions but not the 4
  condition

\NormalTok{cdata8$age_group =}\StringTok{ "old"}
\NormalTok{cdata8$age_group[}\KeywordTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(cdata8$id)) <}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{] =}\StringTok{ "young"}

                    \DataTypeTok{n =} \KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(n),}

                    \DataTypeTok{sd =} \KeywordTok{mean}\NormalTok{(sd),}
                    \DataTypeTok{se =} \KeywordTok{mean}\NormalTok{(se))}

\subsection{Hidden probability}\label{hidden-probability}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# generate orders}
\NormalTok{aap <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{seq}\NormalTok{(.}\DecValTok{075}\NormalTok{, .}\DecValTok{6}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{by =} \NormalTok{.}\DecValTok{075}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{# pilot 3}
\NormalTok{x <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{combinat:::}\KeywordTok{permn}\NormalTok{(aap) }\CommentTok{# all possible permutations}
\NormalTok{select <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sample}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{factorial}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{), }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{replace =} \OtherTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{# select 8}
\NormalTok{ok <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{x[select]}
\NormalTok{df8 <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{do.call}\NormalTok{(rbind.data.frame, ok)}
\KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(df8) <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{# write.table(df8, "../processed/orders8.txt", sep = "\textbackslash{}t", }
  \CommentTok{# quote = F, row.names = F, col.names = T)}
\NormalTok{df8 <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{read.table}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"../processed/orders8.txt"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{header =} \NormalTok{T)}
\NormalTok{for(i in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{) \{}
  \NormalTok{df <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{ID=}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{))}

  \NormalTok{df$Prob2 <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{-df$Prob1}
  \CommentTok{# file <- paste("/materials/conditions/cond_", i*2-1, "_param_4.csv", sep = "")}

\NormalTok{order <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{36}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ncol =} \DecValTok{16}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{trialnr <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{36}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ncol =} \DecValTok{16}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{for(i in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{36}\NormalTok{) \{}
  \NormalTok{if((((i}\DecValTok{-1}\NormalTok{) %%}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{) <}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{T) \{}
    \NormalTok{order[i,] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{16}\NormalTok{)}
    \NormalTok{for(j in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{16}\NormalTok{) \{}
      \NormalTok{trialnr[i,j] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{j}
    \NormalTok{\}}
  \NormalTok{\} }
  \NormalTok{else \{}
    \NormalTok{order[i,] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{16}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
    \NormalTok{for(j in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{16}\NormalTok{) \{}
      \NormalTok{trialnr[i,j] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{-j}
      \NormalTok{if (}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{-j <=}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) trialnr[i,j] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{-j) +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{16}
\CommentTok{#       trialnr[i,j] <- 16-j}
\CommentTok{#       if (16-j <= 0) trialnr[i,j] <- (16-j) + 16 # last trial is always 16}
    \NormalTok{\}}
  \NormalTok{\}}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\NormalTok{dflist =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{list.files}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{pattern=}\StringTok{"*param_4"}\NormalTok{), read.table, }\DataTypeTok{header =} \NormalTok{T, }\DataTypeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
\KeywordTok{setwd}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(home,rmd, }\DataTypeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{))}

\CommentTok{# load randomly generated file with bandit orders}
\NormalTok{df4 <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{read.table}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"../processed/orders4.txt"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{header =} \NormalTok{T)}
\NormalTok{i =}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}
\NormalTok{for (i in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(dflist)) \{}
  \NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$inc <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{i*}\DecValTok{2-1} \CommentTok{# add 8 uneven block_id's 1,3,...,15}
  \NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$dec <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{i*}\DecValTok{2} \CommentTok{# add 8 even block_id's 2,4,...,16}
  \NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$i <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{i }\CommentTok{# add counter 1-8}
  \CommentTok{# lookup order from orders4.txt, which is unnecessary}
  \NormalTok{order8 <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$Prob1 }
  \NormalTok{row =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{()}
  \NormalTok{for(j in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df4)) \{}
    \CommentTok{# check which row has the same order}
    \NormalTok{row[j] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{all}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(df4[j,] ) ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{order8) }
  \NormalTok{\}}
  \KeywordTok{row.names}\NormalTok{(df4[row,])}
  \CommentTok{# add "order" from genfile to cond orders}
  \CommentTok{# indicates another randomly generated problem ID}
  \NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$order8 <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{row.names}\NormalTok{(df4[row,])) }
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{log$block_size =}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}
\NormalTok{cond_4 <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{log}

\KeywordTok{setwd}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(home,change, }\DataTypeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{for (i in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(dflist)) \{}
  \NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$inc <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{i*}\DecValTok{2}
  \NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$dec <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{i*}\DecValTok{2-1}

  \NormalTok{order8 <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$Prob1}

  \NormalTok{for(j in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df8)) \{}

  \NormalTok{\}}
  \KeywordTok{row.names}\NormalTok{(df4[row,])}
  \NormalTok{dflist[[i]]$order8 <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{row.names}\NormalTok{(df8[row,]))}
\NormalTok{\}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{cond <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(cond_4, cond_8)}
\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cond)[}\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cond)==}\StringTok{"ID"}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "bandit_id"} \CommentTok{# as based on cond files}
\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cond)[}\KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(cond)==}\StringTok{"i"}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "block_size_id8"} \CommentTok{# order based on condition files}

\CommentTok{# determine 1-8 bandit id's (same as bandit_id as based on condition files + 1)}
\NormalTok{cond$bandit_real_id[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{) }
\NormalTok{cond$bandit_real_id[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{) }

\CommentTok{# determine 1-16 instead of 1-8 order number for both conditions based on orders.txt}
\NormalTok{cond$order <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cond$order8 }
\NormalTok{cond$order16[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(cond$order8[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{] *}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) -}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}
\NormalTok{cond$order16[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cond$order8[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{] *}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}

\CommentTok{# determine 1-16 instead of 1-8 order number for both conditions based on orders.txt}
\NormalTok{cond$block_size_id <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cond$block_size_id8}
\NormalTok{cond$block_size_id16[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{    }\NormalTok{(cond$block_size_id8[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{] *}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{) -}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}
\NormalTok{cond$block_size_id16[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{    }\NormalTok{cond$block_size_id8[cond$block_size ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{] *}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}
\NormalTok{log <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cond}
\CommentTok{# log}
\CommentTok{# block_size_id's are based on cond param files}
\CommentTok{# order id's are based on orders.txt files}

                 \DataTypeTok{by.x =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"bandit_id"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"order"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"block_size"}\NormalTok{), }

\subsection{Regret}\label{regret}

\subsection{Regret}\label{regret-1}

\subsubsection{Regret across
participants}\label{regret-across-participants}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{regret <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(choices) \{ }
    \KeywordTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{cumsum}\NormalTok{(W_OPT -}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.double}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(choices))))}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{getScheme <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(game, N_BANDITS, basescheme) \{}
    \CommentTok{# trial numbers of first time choice for each bandit}
    \NormalTok{oc        <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{match}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(game$bandit_real_id), game$bandit_real_id) }
    \NormalTok{newscheme <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{cbind}\NormalTok{(game$ev[oc],   game$bandit_real_id[oc]))}
    \NormalTok{scheme    <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{merge}\NormalTok{(basescheme, newscheme, }\DataTypeTok{by.x =} \StringTok{"ev"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{by.y =} \StringTok{"V1"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{all.x =} \NormalTok{T)}
    \NormalTok{scheme    <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{scheme[}\KeywordTok{order}\NormalTok{(scheme[,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{decreasing =} \OtherTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{),]}
    \NormalTok{scheme$evorder <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:N_BANDITS}
    \NormalTok{scheme    <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{scheme[}\KeywordTok{order}\NormalTok{(scheme[,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{decreasing =} \OtherTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{),]}
    \NormalTok{scheme$V2[}\KeywordTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(scheme$V2)] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:N_BANDITS)[(scheme$V2 %in%}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:N_BANDITS) ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{F]}
    \KeywordTok{return}\NormalTok{(scheme)}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\NormalTok{for(i in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$age_group))) \{}
  \NormalTok{for(pp in }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$id[data$age_group ==}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$age_group)[i]])) \{}
    \NormalTok{for(tr in }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$block_id[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{pp])) \{}
      \NormalTok{evchoices =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$ev[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{pp &}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$block_id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tr] }

        \NormalTok{tr, }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$block_id[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{pp])}

    \NormalTok{for(tr in }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$block_id[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{pp])) \{}
      \NormalTok{evchoices =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$ev[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{pp &}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$block_id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tr] }
      \NormalTok{game_regret =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{regret}\NormalTok{(evchoices)}
      \NormalTok{data$regret[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{pp &}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data$block_id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tr] =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{game_regret}
    \NormalTok{\}}
    \NormalTok{id =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{id +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}
\NormalTok{\} }

                    \DataTypeTok{sd.sc =} \KeywordTok{mean}\NormalTok{(sd.sc),}
                    \DataTypeTok{se =} \KeywordTok{mean}\NormalTok{(se))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section{Computational}\label{computational}

\newpage

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{bbanditsfunc <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(param, game, N_BANDITS) \{}
    \NormalTok{theta =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{param[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
    \NormalTok{lik <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} 
    \NormalTok{bantrials <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ncol =} \NormalTok{N_BANDITS) }
    \NormalTok{wins      <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ncol =} \NormalTok{N_BANDITS) }
    
    \NormalTok{if ((theta <}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{0.005}\NormalTok{) |}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(theta >}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{30}\NormalTok{)) \{}
        \NormalTok{LL <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{-}\DecValTok{999999}   
    \NormalTok{\} }
    \NormalTok{else \{}
        \NormalTok{for (trial in }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{99}\NormalTok{)) \{}
            \NormalTok{choice <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{game$bandit_real_id[game$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{trial]}
            \NormalTok{R      <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{game$payoff        [game$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{trial]}
            \NormalTok{probs <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{getProbs}\NormalTok{(wins, bantrials, theta, lik)}
            \NormalTok{b =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{probs[choice]}
            \NormalTok{if (}\KeywordTok{is.nan}\NormalTok{(b))                      \{b <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1} \NormalTok{/}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{MIN_GRAIN\}}
            \NormalTok{if (b <=}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1} \NormalTok{/}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{MIN_GRAIN))           \{b <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1} \NormalTok{/}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{MIN_GRAIN\}}
            \NormalTok{if (b >=}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(MIN_GRAIN -}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)/MIN_GRAIN) \{b <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{\}}
            \NormalTok{lik =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{lik +}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{log}\NormalTok{(b)}
            \NormalTok{wins     [choice] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{wins     [choice] +}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{R}
            \NormalTok{bantrials[choice] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{bantrials[choice] +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}
        \NormalTok{\}}
    \NormalTok{\}}
    \KeywordTok{return}\NormalTok{(-lik)}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\CommentTok{# predict and hist plots}
\NormalTok{getParams <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(data, bbanditsfunc) \{}
    \NormalTok{subjects =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$id)}
    
    \NormalTok{fi_bb <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }
        \DataTypeTok{nrow =} \KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subjects)), }
        \DataTypeTok{ncol =} \DecValTok{6}\NormalTok{)}
    \NormalTok{fi_bb[,}\DecValTok{6}\NormalTok{] =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{subjects}
    
    \NormalTok{for (id in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subjects))) \{  }
        \KeywordTok{print}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"id  "}\NormalTok{, id))}
        \NormalTok{subdata <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subjects)[id],]}

        \NormalTok{bb.lik <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \OtherTok{NA}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ncol =} \NormalTok{MAXITERBB) }
        \NormalTok{bb.tht <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \OtherTok{NA}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ncol =} \NormalTok{MAXITERBB) }

        \NormalTok{for (games in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$block_id[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subjects)[id]]))) \{}
            \KeywordTok{print}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"game"}\NormalTok{, games))}
            \NormalTok{gamedata =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{subdata[subdata$block_id ==}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subdata$block_id)[games],]}
            
            \NormalTok{if (MAXITERBB >}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{) \{}
                \NormalTok{for (iter in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:MAXITERBB) \{}
                    \NormalTok{startParm <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{runif}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(BB.LB)) *}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(BB.UB -}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{BB.LB) +}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{BB.LB }
                    \KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(startParm) <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"theta"}\NormalTok{)}
                    \NormalTok{out <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{optim}\NormalTok{(startParm, bbanditsfunc, }\DataTypeTok{game =} \NormalTok{gamedata, }
                                 \DataTypeTok{N_BANDITS =} \NormalTok{N_BANDITS, }
                                 \DataTypeTok{method =} \StringTok{"L-BFGS-B"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{lower =} \NormalTok{BB.LB, }\DataTypeTok{upper =} \NormalTok{BB.UB)}
                    \NormalTok{whle =}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0}
                    \NormalTok{while (out$value ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{&}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{whle <}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{WHLEBB) \{}
                        \CommentTok{# subst BB.UB with 1 to a bit focus less on randomness?}
                        \NormalTok{startParm <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{runif}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(BB.LB)) *}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1} \NormalTok{-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{BB.LB) +}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{BB.LB }
                        \KeywordTok{names}\NormalTok{(startParm) <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"theta"}\NormalTok{)}
                        \NormalTok{out <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{optim}\NormalTok{(startParm, bbanditsfunc, }\DataTypeTok{game =} \NormalTok{gamedata, }
                                     \DataTypeTok{N_BANDITS =} \NormalTok{N_BANDITS, }
                                     \DataTypeTok{method =} \StringTok{"L-BFGS-B"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{lower =} \NormalTok{BB.LB, }\DataTypeTok{upper =} \NormalTok{BB.UB)}
                        \NormalTok{whle =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{whle +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}
                        \CommentTok{# print(paste("whle", whle, "tht", round(startParm, digits = 1)))}
                    \NormalTok{\}}
                    \NormalTok{if(out$value ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{|}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{out$value >}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{300}\NormalTok{) \{}
                        \NormalTok{out$value =}\StringTok{ }\OtherTok{NA}
                        \KeywordTok{print}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"OUT VALUE IS IMPOSSIBLE"}\NormalTok{, id, games, }\DataTypeTok{sep =} \StringTok{" "}\NormalTok{))}
                    \NormalTok{\}}
                    \KeywordTok{print}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"BB "}\NormalTok{, }
                                \KeywordTok{round}\NormalTok{(out$value, }\DataTypeTok{digits =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{), }
                                \KeywordTok{round}\NormalTok{(out$par[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{digits =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)))}
                    \NormalTok{bb.lik[games,iter] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{out$value}
                    \NormalTok{bb.tht[games,iter] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{out$par[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
                \NormalTok{\}}
            \NormalTok{\}}
        \NormalTok{\}}
        \NormalTok{if (MAXITERBB >}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{) \{}
            \NormalTok{fi_bb[id,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{median}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{apply}\NormalTok{(bb.lik,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,min), }\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \NormalTok{T)}
            \NormalTok{fi_bb[id,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{median}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{apply}\NormalTok{(bb.tht,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,min), }\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \NormalTok{T)}
            \NormalTok{fi_bb[id,}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{median}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{apply}\NormalTok{(bb.tht,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,min), }\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \NormalTok{T)}
        \NormalTok{\}}
    \NormalTok{\}}
    
    \NormalTok{fi_bb[,}\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2} \NormalTok{*}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{fi_bb[,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2} \NormalTok{*}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{log}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{# BIC: deviance + #parameters * log(N)}
    \NormalTok{fi_bb[,}\DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2} \NormalTok{*}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{fi_bb[,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2} \NormalTok{*}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}        \CommentTok{# AIC: deviance + #parameters * 2}
    \NormalTok{fi_bb}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{getPredictions <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(data, fi_bb) \{}
    \NormalTok{subjects =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(fi_bb[,}\DecValTok{6}\NormalTok{])}

    \NormalTok{basescheme =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{sort}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$ev)));}
    \KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(basescheme)[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ "ev"}
    
    \CommentTok{# 3D array subjects, trials, 8 (q values per trial and choices)}
    \NormalTok{pr_bb <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{array}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \OtherTok{NA}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{dim =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(subjects)*}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{*N_BANDITS)) }
    \NormalTok{for (id in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subjects)))\{}
        \NormalTok{thetaBB <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{fi_bb[id,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{];}
        \NormalTok{subdata =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subjects)[id],]}
        \NormalTok{for (games in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data$block_id[data$id ==}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subjects)[id]]))) \{}
            \NormalTok{gamedata =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{subdata[subdata$block_id ==}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(subdata$block_id)[games],]}
            \NormalTok{scheme <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{getScheme}\NormalTok{(gamedata, N_BANDITS, basescheme) }
            \NormalTok{bantrials <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ncol =} \NormalTok{N_BANDITS) }
            \NormalTok{wins      <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ncol =} \NormalTok{N_BANDITS) }
            
            \NormalTok{for (trial in }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{99}\NormalTok{)) \{}
                \NormalTok{choice <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{gamedata$bandit_real_id[gamedata$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{trial]}
                \NormalTok{R      <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{gamedata$payoff        [gamedata$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{trial]}
                \NormalTok{ev     <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{gamedata$ev            [gamedata$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{trial]}
                
                \CommentTok{# BB}
                \NormalTok{probs <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{getProbs}\NormalTok{(wins, bantrials, thetaBB)}
                \NormalTok{orderedprobs =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{probs[}\KeywordTok{order}\NormalTok{(scheme$evorder, }\DataTypeTok{decreasing =} \OtherTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)]}
                \NormalTok{ind <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{which}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{sort}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(gamedata$ev)) ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{ev)}
                \NormalTok{pr_bb[(id -}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) *}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8} \NormalTok{+}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{games, trial +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:N_BANDITS] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{orderedprobs}
                \NormalTok{pr_bb[(id -}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) *}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8} \NormalTok{+}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{games, trial +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, N_BANDITS +}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{ind] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}
                \NormalTok{wins     [choice] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{wins     [choice] +}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{R}
                \NormalTok{bantrials[choice] <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{bantrials[choice] +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}
            \NormalTok{\}}
        \NormalTok{\}}
    \NormalTok{\}  }
    \CommentTok{# print(colMeans(pr_bb, dims = 1, na.rm = T))}
    \NormalTok{pr_bb}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{colSeColMeans <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(x, }\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \NormalTok{if (na.rm) \{ }
        \NormalTok{n <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{colSums}\NormalTok{(!}\KeywordTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(x)) }
        \NormalTok{p <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{colMeans}\NormalTok{(x, }\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \NormalTok{T)}
    \NormalTok{\} }
    \NormalTok{else \{}
        \NormalTok{n <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(x) }
        \NormalTok{p <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{colMeans}\NormalTok{(x)}
    \NormalTok{\}}
    \KeywordTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{((}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{/n) *}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{p *}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{-p)))}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{plottrialsSE <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(aggrPROB, BIC, group, lgnd, ylb, }\DataTypeTok{model =} \StringTok{"predicted"}\NormalTok{, }
                         \DataTypeTok{col_se =} \KeywordTok{array}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{dim =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{*N_BANDITS))) \{}

    \NormalTok{\}}
    \NormalTok{xl <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{seq}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{min}\NormalTok{(x),}\KeywordTok{max}\NormalTok{(x), (}\KeywordTok{max}\NormalTok{(x) -}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{min}\NormalTok{(x))/}\DecValTok{1000}\NormalTok{)}

    \NormalTok{if (N_BANDITS ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{) \{}

        \KeywordTok{lines}\NormalTok{(xl, }\KeywordTok{predict}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{loess}\NormalTok{(aggrPROB[,N_BANDITS +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{6}\NormalTok{] +}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{col_se[,N_BANDITS +}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{6}\NormalTok{] ~x, }

\NormalTok{plottrials <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(aggrPROB, BIC, group, lgnd, ylb, }\DataTypeTok{model =} \StringTok{"predicted"}\NormalTok{, }
                       \DataTypeTok{col_se =} \KeywordTok{array}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{data =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{dim =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{*N_BANDITS))) \{}
    \NormalTok{sp =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{.}\DecValTok{4} \CommentTok{# % of the points}
    \NormalTok{colors =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{rainbow}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{n =} \DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{start=}\NormalTok{.}\DecValTok{7}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{end=}\NormalTok{.}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{my_gg_plot <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(data, cdata, var, xlab, color_choose, limits_choose, }
                       \NormalTok{breaks_choose, labels_choose)\{}
    \NormalTok{data$temp <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data[,var]}
    \NormalTok{data <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data[}\KeywordTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(data$temp)==}\OtherTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{,]}

                       \DataTypeTok{position =} \StringTok{"identity"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{binwidth =} \DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{) +}
\StringTok{        }\KeywordTok{scale_fill_discrete}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{name =} \StringTok{"Age"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{breaks =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{24}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{70}\NormalTok{), }\DataTypeTok{labels =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"YA"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"OA"}\NormalTok{)) +}
\StringTok{        }\KeywordTok{geom_vline}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{xintercept=}\NormalTok{likBB_median.median, }\DataTypeTok{colour=}\NormalTok{age),}
                   \DataTypeTok{data=}\NormalTok{cdata, }\DataTypeTok{linetype=}\StringTok{"dashed"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{size=}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }
                   \DataTypeTok{alpha =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{show.legend =} \OtherTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{) +}
\StringTok{        }\KeywordTok{scale_y_continuous}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, }

\subsection{Visual model comparison}\label{visual-model-comparison}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# load fits}
\NormalTok{data4 <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{read.table}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{file =} \StringTok{"../processed/B-4-options-median.csv"}\NormalTok{, }
                   \DataTypeTok{quote =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{sep =} \StringTok{","}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{header =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{data8 <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{read.table}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{file =} \StringTok{"../processed/B-8-options-median.csv"}\NormalTok{, }
                   \DataTypeTok{quote =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{sep =} \StringTok{","}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{header =} \OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{data4$age <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(data4$age)}
\NormalTok{data8$age <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(data8$age)}
\KeywordTok{summary}\NormalTok{(data4)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\NormalTok{dataall <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{dataall[, }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"id"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"bandit_real_id"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"payoff"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"trial_number"}\NormalTok{, }
                       \StringTok{"block_id"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"ev"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"block_size"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"age_group"}\NormalTok{)]}

\NormalTok{BB.LB =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\FloatTok{0.005}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{# theta}
\NormalTok{BB.UB =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{30}\NormalTok{)    }\CommentTok{# theta}

\NormalTok{filename =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"../processed/BBresults"}\NormalTok{, N_BANDITS, }\StringTok{"N"}\NormalTok{, group, ex, }\StringTok{".RData"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{sep=} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}

\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

    \NormalTok{preds[, , }\DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{][}\KeywordTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(preds[, , }\DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{])] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0}

\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{agse.predsYA <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{apply}\NormalTok{(preds, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, colSeColMeans, }\DataTypeTok{na.rm =} \NormalTok{T) }
\end{Highlighting}

\section{Individual plots}\label{individual-plots}

\subsection{Individual proportions}\label{individual-proportions}

\newpage

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{load}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"../processed/data.ev.test-final.RData"}\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{# unique(data.ev.test$id)}
\NormalTok{tgc <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{summarySE}\NormalTok{(data.ev.test, }\DataTypeTok{measurevar=}\StringTok{"ev.prop"}\NormalTok{, }
                 \DataTypeTok{groupvars=}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"id"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"age_group"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"block_size"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"ev"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{tgc$ev.prop <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tgc$sum /}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}

\NormalTok{for (i in }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data.ev.test$id)) \{}
    \NormalTok{pd <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{position_dodge}\NormalTok{(}\FloatTok{0.6}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{# move them .05 to the left and right}
    \NormalTok{chart_title <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Proportions for participant number "}\NormalTok{,i,}\StringTok{"."}\NormalTok{,}\DataTypeTok{sep=}\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
    \NormalTok{p <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{ggplot}\NormalTok{(tgc[tgc$id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{i,], }\KeywordTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{x =} \NormalTok{ev, }\DataTypeTok{y =} \NormalTok{ev.prop, }\DataTypeTok{fill =} \NormalTok{age_group)) +}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{        }\KeywordTok{geom_bar}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{position=}\NormalTok{pd, }\DataTypeTok{stat=}\StringTok{"identity"}\NormalTok{) +}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{        }\KeywordTok{geom_errorbar}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{ymax=}\NormalTok{ev.prop+se , }\DataTypeTok{ymin=} \NormalTok{ev.prop-se), }
                      \DataTypeTok{width =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{position =} \NormalTok{pd) +}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{        }\KeywordTok{facet_wrap}\NormalTok{(~}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{block_size) +}\StringTok{ }
\StringTok{        }\KeywordTok{scale_y_continuous}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{breaks=}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{*}\DecValTok{20}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{limits =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{)) +}
\StringTok{        }\KeywordTok{labs}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{x=}\StringTok{"Expected value"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{y=}\StringTok{"Average proportion"}\NormalTok{, }
             \DataTypeTok{title=}\NormalTok{chart_title, }\DataTypeTok{fill =} \StringTok{"Age"}\NormalTok{)}
    \CommentTok{# ggsave("ev_pilot2_error_bars.png", width = 6, height = 4)}
    \KeywordTok{print}\NormalTok{(p) }
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsection{Choice profiles}\label{choice-profiles}

A simple way to look at sequential sampling data\textsuperscript{1,2}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# choices is vector of all choices, }
\CommentTok{# numbers should represent the order of the hidden probabilities}
\NormalTok{W_OPT =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{.}\DecValTok{6}
\NormalTok{regret <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{function(choices) \{ }
    \KeywordTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{cumsum}\NormalTok{(W_OPT -}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.double}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(choices))))}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{load}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"../processed/data.ev-final.RData"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{for(i in }\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data.ev$id)) \{}
    \NormalTok{for(j in }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data.ev$block_id))) \{}
        \CommentTok{#     i = 1}
        \CommentTok{#     j = 8}
        \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{newpage}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
        \NormalTok{problem <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data.ev[data.ev$block_id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{j &}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{data.ev$id ==}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{i,]}
        \KeywordTok{print}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"id: "}\NormalTok{, i }
                    \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{", gender: "}\NormalTok{, problem$gender[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] }
                    \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{", age: "}\NormalTok{, problem$age[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] }
                    \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{", block: "}\NormalTok{, j }
                    \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{", total: "}\NormalTok{, problem$block_score[problem$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{99}\NormalTok{]}
                    \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{))}
        \KeywordTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\CharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
        
        \NormalTok{banditcnt <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{problem$block_size[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
        \NormalTok{evs <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sort}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unique}\NormalTok{(data.ev$ev))  }
        \NormalTok{if(problem$block_size[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{) \{evs <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{evs[}\DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{]\}}
        \NormalTok{ev_positions =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{match}\NormalTok{(problem$ev, evs)    }
        
        \NormalTok{ttlrgrt =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{round}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{tail}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{regret}\NormalTok{(problem$ev), }\DataTypeTok{n =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{), }\DataTypeTok{digits =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
        \NormalTok{pnts =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{problem$block_score[problem$trial_number ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{99}\NormalTok{]    }
        \CommentTok{# pdf(paste(}
        \CommentTok{#       "Total regret of ",}
        \CommentTok{#       ttlrgrt}
        \CommentTok{#       , " points"}
        \CommentTok{#       , " by a ", problem$age[1]}
        \CommentTok{#       , " year old "}
        \CommentTok{#       , problem$gender[1]}
        \CommentTok{#       , " (id ", i}
        \CommentTok{#       , ", gm ", j}
        \CommentTok{#       , ").pdf"}
        \CommentTok{#       , sep = ""), }
        \CommentTok{#   width=inch_width, }
        \CommentTok{#   height=inch_height, }
        \CommentTok{#   pointsize = pointsize)}
        \KeywordTok{plot}\NormalTok{(ev_positions,  }
             \DataTypeTok{type=}\StringTok{"l"}\NormalTok{, }\CommentTok{# lines and dots}
             \DataTypeTok{bty=}\StringTok{"n"}\NormalTok{,  }\CommentTok{# supresses box }
             \DataTypeTok{axes=}\NormalTok{F,  }
             \DataTypeTok{ylab=}\StringTok{"Hidden probabilities"}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{xlab=}\StringTok{"Trial number"}\NormalTok{, }
             \DataTypeTok{cex.lab=}\FloatTok{1.4}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{lwd=}\FloatTok{1.5}\NormalTok{) }
        
        \KeywordTok{levels}\NormalTok{(evs) <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"0.0"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{".0"}\NormalTok{, }\KeywordTok{levels}\NormalTok{(tgc$ev))}
        \KeywordTok{levels}\NormalTok{(evs) <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"0."}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"."}\NormalTok{, }\KeywordTok{levels}\NormalTok{(tgc$ev))}
        \KeywordTok{levels}\NormalTok{(evs)[}\KeywordTok{levels}\NormalTok{(tgc$ev)==}\StringTok{"..5"}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ ".075"}
        \NormalTok{if(problem$block_size[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{) \{}\KeywordTok{levels}\NormalTok{(evs)[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ ".075"}\NormalTok{\}}
        \KeywordTok{axis}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{at=}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{*}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{cex.axis=}\FloatTok{1.2}\NormalTok{) }
        \KeywordTok{axis}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{at=}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:(banditcnt),  }\DataTypeTok{label =} \KeywordTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(evs), }\DataTypeTok{las=}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{cex.axis=}\FloatTok{1.2}\NormalTok{)  }
        \KeywordTok{points}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{x =} \KeywordTok{which}\NormalTok{(problem$payoff ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{%in%}\StringTok{ }\OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{), }
               \DataTypeTok{y =} \NormalTok{ev_positions[problem$payoff ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{col =} \StringTok{"red"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{pch =} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{)}
        \KeywordTok{points}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{x =} \KeywordTok{which}\NormalTok{(problem$payoff ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1} \NormalTok{%in%}\StringTok{ }\OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{), }
               \DataTypeTok{y =} \NormalTok{ev_positions[problem$payoff ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{col =} \StringTok{"green"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{pch =} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{)}
        \KeywordTok{title}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}
            \StringTok{"Total regret of "}\NormalTok{, }
            \NormalTok{ttlrgrt}
            \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" points"}
            \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" by a "}\NormalTok{, problem$age[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]     }
            \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" year old "}
            \NormalTok{, problem$gender[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] }
            \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{" (id "}\NormalTok{, i }
            \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{", gm "}\NormalTok{, j}
            \NormalTok{, }\StringTok{")"}
            \NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{sep =} \StringTok{""}\NormalTok{))}
        
        \CommentTok{#     dev.off()}
        
        \CommentTok{# Reaction Time}
        \NormalTok{problem$rt[problem$rt >}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}
        \KeywordTok{plot}\NormalTok{(problem$rt,  }
             \DataTypeTok{type=}\StringTok{"l"}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{bty=}\StringTok{"n"}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{axes=}\NormalTok{F,  }\DataTypeTok{ylab=}\StringTok{"Reaction Time"}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{xlab=}\StringTok{"Trial"}\NormalTok{, }
             \DataTypeTok{cex.lab=}\FloatTok{1.4}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{lwd=}\FloatTok{1.5}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{ylim =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)) }
        \KeywordTok{points}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{x =} \KeywordTok{which}\NormalTok{(problem$payoff ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0} \NormalTok{%in%}\StringTok{ }\OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{), }
               \DataTypeTok{y =} \NormalTok{problem$rt[problem$payoff ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{col =} \StringTok{"red"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{pch =} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{)}
        \KeywordTok{points}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{x =} \KeywordTok{which}\NormalTok{(problem$payoff ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1} \NormalTok{%in%}\StringTok{ }\OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{), }
               \DataTypeTok{y =} \NormalTok{problem$rt[problem$payoff ==}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\DataTypeTok{col =} \StringTok{"green"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{pch =} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{)}
        \KeywordTok{axis}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{at=}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{*}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{cex.axis=}\FloatTok{1.2}\NormalTok{) }
        \KeywordTok{axis}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{at=}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{las=}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{,  }\DataTypeTok{cex.axis=}\FloatTok{1.2}\NormalTok{) }
        \CommentTok{# (((round(min(problem$rt), 1)-0)*1):((round(max(problem$rt), 1)+1)*1))/1}
    \NormalTok{\}}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
